 uttar pradesh police hitech hone ja rahi he
 Now any order issued from the Directorate General level to the soldiers will come directly through SMS on their mobiles
 police mahanideshaalay ne sabhi sipaahiyon ke mobile or pieno number juta liye hai
 Orders issued from the Directorate General of Police are usually sent at the police station level and every soldier is given information about it
 aksar aisa bhi hota he ki aadesh sipaahiyon tak pahunch nahin paata he
 To overcome this problem, SMS service is being started from the state level under the new scheme
 koi bhi nayaa aadesh police mahanideshaalay se i-mail ke jariye jila mukhyalay ke control room ke computer par bheja jayega
 The mobile and PNO numbers of the soldiers from all over the district will be fed on the computer of every police control room and in just one click the message will reach the soldiers' mobiles through SMS

 rajasthan royles team ne ravivaar ko savai maansingh stadium main khele gaye indian premier lig (ipel) ke chathe sanskaran ke 61wein mukaable main do baar ke champion chennai super kings ko paanch wicket se haraakar nau tiimon kii talika main doosraa sthaan hasil kar liya he
 Rajasthan won all eight matches played at their home ground thanks to the brilliant batting of Shane Watson (70) and Stuart Binny (41 not out)
 toss harkar pehle ballebaaji karne utari super kings ne murali vijay ke 55 or maaikel hasi ke 40 ranon kii badaulat rajasthan royles ke saamne 142 ranon kaa lakshya rakhaa tha, jise usne paanch wicket khokar 17
 Achieved in 1 over only
 binni ne apni 23 gendon kii naabad pari main do chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 Watson, who was elected man of the match, hit six fours and six sixes off 34 balls
 binni or watson ke bich paanchaven wicket ke liye 45 gendon par 93 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Rajasthan lost the wickets of Rahul Dravid (22), Ajinkya Rahane (9), James Faulkner (1) and Sanju Samson (0) apart from Watson
 ek samay mejabaan team ne 45 ranon par chaar wicket ganvaa die the
 By this time, the Super Kings had a hold on the match, but after this, Watson and Binny played with restraint to bring their team to victory
 super kings kii ore se jesan holder ne do wicket liye
 Rajasthan have won 20 out of 14 matches and scored 20 points
 vah talika main duusare kram par he
 The Super Kings also have 20 points in their account but their net run rate is better than Rajasthan and that is why they are first in the table
 mumbai indiens 18 ankon ke saath tisare kram par hai
 After the match, Rajasthan players made rounds of the field to thank their domestic supporters
 samarthakon ne unka joardaar abhinandan kiya
 Rajasthan has finally set a record by winning all their home matches in IPL-6
 isse pehle, super kings ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chaar wicket par 141 ran banaae
 This includes Murali Vijay's 55, Michael Hussey's 40 and Dwayne Bravo's 23 not out
 super kings ne behad sadhi shuruyaat kii lekin 11wein over ke baad teen wicket jaldi-jaldi girane ke kaaran madhya main uskaa khel dhimaa ho gaya
 Super Kings added 25 runs in the last two overs to complete it and scored 141 runs for the loss of four wickets in the prescribed 20 overs
 super kings ne rajasthan ke khilaaf pehle wicket ke liye sabase badi saajhedaari kii
 Michael Hussey (40) added 83 runs for the first wicket with Murali Vijay
 hasi ko 12wein over kii teesri gend par stuart binni ne bold kiya
 Hussey faced 40 balls and hit six fours
 haalanki iske baad achche form main chal rahe suresh raina or captain mahendra singh dhoni behtareen shuruyaat kaa phayda nahin uthaa sake

 saath hi notebandi par supreme court ne sunwaayee ke dauraan centre se poocha ki kya is maamle main koi ricard he? notebandi se pehle dimag lagaaya gaya ki isse kitni karency waapas aegi? kaise nai karency chhaapi jaaegi? kya iske liye koi yojana thi? sarkaar ko notebandi ke faisle se kya ummiden thim? During the hearing, the Supreme Court had asked the Center whether the court should set a minimum limit for withdrawing money from the bank which is applicable across the country and there is no discrimination
 sarkaar ne 24 hajaar kii limit tay kii lekin bank logon ko itnaa bhi nahin de paa rahe

 court ne poocha ki logon se kiya vaayada puraa hona chahie
 On this, the Attorney General (AG) has been asked by the government and asked for the answer
 iske saath hi notebandi maamle main supreme court ne sunwaayee ke liye mudde taiyaar kiye, court ne kaha in sawaalon par hi hogi sunwaayee : 1
 notebandi kaa faisla RBI act 26 (2) kaa ulanghan he? jisamen kaha gaya he ki kendriya board kii manjuuri se ye kiya ja saktaa he or kisi siries ke noton ko band kiya ja saktaa he
 2
 notebandi kaa 8 november or uske baad ke notification asanvaidhanik hai? 3
 notebandi samvidhan ke die samanta ke adhikaar anuchhed 14 or vyapaar karne kii aazaadee se sambandhit anuchhed 19 jaise moulik adhikaron kaa ulanghan hai? 4
 notebandi ke faisle ko bina taiyaari ke saath lagu kiya gaya jabaki naa to nai karency kaa sahi intjaam tha or naa hi desh bhar main cash pahunchane kaa? 5
 bainkon or ATM se paisa nikaalane kii seemaa tay karnaa logon ke adhikaron kaa hanan he ? 6 Is it not right to stop depositing old notes in district cooperative banks and withdrawing new rupees? 7
 Can a political party file a petition in the Supreme Court under a public interest litigation? sunwaayee ke dauraan centre sarkaar kii ore se AG mukul rohtagi ne sawaal uthaaya ki CPM jaisi raajnneetik party kaise janhit yachika daakhil kar sakati he? chif justise thakur ne kaha ki wo is maamle kii sunwaayee bhi karenge

 is par atorni general (AG) se sarkaar se puch kar jawaab maanga he
 With this, the Supreme Court prepared the issues for hearing in the demonetization case, the court said that these questions will be heard only: 1
 Is the decision on demonetisation a violation of RBI Act 26 (2)? In which it is said that this can be done with the approval of the Central Board and the notes of any series can be closed
 2
 Are demonetization notifications on November 8 and beyond unconstitutional? 3
 Demonetisation is a violation of fundamental rights such as Article 14 of the Constitution's right to equality and Article 19 relating to freedom of doing business? 4
 The decision of demonetisation was implemented with no preparation, while neither the new currency was properly arranged nor the cash was circulated across the country? 5
 Is the right to withdraw money from banks and atms a violation of people's rights? 6 jila sahakaari bainko main puraane note jamaa karne or nae rupee nikaalane par roak sahi nahin he? 7
 koi raajnneetik party janhit ke yachika ke tahat supreme court main daakhil kar sakati he ? During the hearing, on behalf of the central government, AG Mukul Rohatgi raised the question that how can a political party like CPM file a PIL? Chief Justice Thakur said that he would also hear the case
 centre ne supreme court ko bataaya ab tak 12 lakh karod kii puraani karency jamaa ho chuki he
 p Chidambaram said that the way the arrangements are made, it is clear that it will take five months for the government to print a new currency
 supreme court notebandi maamle main ahm sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 During the last hearing, the Supreme Court had asked the government to consider the demand for cooperative banks, stating that they have not been allowed to conduct banking operations
 kooparative bainkon kii ore se kaha gaya he ki unhen banking transction kii ijaajat nahin di gai he is kaaran graahakon ko mushkil ho rahi he or jo bhi khatadharak hai unhen pareshaani kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he wo na to paise nikaal paa rahe hai or na hi jamaa kar paa rahe hai
 During the hearing, co-operative banks in Kerala and Maharashtra were told that they were unable to make payments to the account holders and were not able to pay pensions due to the lack of permission for banking operations after demonetisation
 8 se 14 november ke bich jo paise jamaa kiye gaye unke bare main kya upaay kiya jaae
 The economy related to the village has reached a high point
 is par supreme court ne atorni general se kaha he ki aap bataaen ki inhen kyon nahin dekh rahe hai
 Then the Attorney General said that his case is also being looked at but the difficulty is that the infrastructure of cooperative banks is not good
 inke paas niyamit bainkon kii tarah computerigeshan se lekar anya suvidhaayen nahin he ki jaali noton kii pahchaan ho sake or blike mani se bachaav ho sake
 In such a situation, these banks have been kept away from banking transactions for the same reason
 tippaniyan At the same time, Senior Advocate P
 presented on behalf of the petitioners
 chidambaram ne kaha ki desh bhar main 371 kooparative bank hai or is kaaran arthvyavastha par asar ho rahaa he
 Meanwhile, the Attorney General raised the issue of transfer of all the cases and said that the petitionation file is being filed in the daily demonetisation case across the country
 desh bhar main aise 70 arji daakhil ho chuke hai, supreme court main 15 argiyaan daakhil kii gai he
 In such a case, all the cases should be transferred to a High Court
 is par chif justise ties thakur ne kaha ki adaalatein hongi or maamle honge to court main log aaenge hi
 With this, the Supreme Court prepared the issues for hearing in the demonetization case, the court said that these questions will be heard only: 1
 Is the decision on demonetisation a violation of RBI Act 26 (2)? In which it is said that this can be done with the approval of the Central Board and the notes of any series can be closed
 2
 Are demonetization notifications on November 8 and beyond unconstitutional? 3
 Demonetisation is a violation of fundamental rights such as Article 14 of the Constitution's right to equality and Article 19 relating to freedom of doing business? 4
 The decision of demonetisation was implemented with no preparation, while neither the new currency was properly arranged nor the cash was circulated across the country? 5
 Is the right to withdraw money from banks and atms a violation of people's rights? 6 jila sahakaari bainko main puraane note jamaa karne or nae rupee nikaalane par roak sahi nahin he? 7
 koi raajnneetik party janhit ke yachika ke tahat supreme court main daakhil kar sakati he ? During the hearing, on behalf of the central government, AG Mukul Rohatgi raised the question that how can a political party like CPM file a PIL? Chief Justice Thakur said that he would also hear the case
 centre ne supreme court ko bataaya ab tak 12 lakh karod kii puraani karency jamaa ho chuki he
 p Chidambaram said that the way the arrangements are made, it is clear that it will take five months for the government to print a new currency
 supreme court notebandi maamle main ahm sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 During the last hearing, the Supreme Court had asked the government to consider the demand for cooperative banks, stating that they have not been allowed to conduct banking operations
 kooparative bainkon kii ore se kaha gaya he ki unhen banking transction kii ijaajat nahin di gai he is kaaran graahakon ko mushkil ho rahi he or jo bhi khatadharak hai unhen pareshaani kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he wo na to paise nikaal paa rahe hai or na hi jamaa kar paa rahe hai
 During the hearing, co-operative banks in Kerala and Maharashtra were told that they were unable to make payments to the account holders and were not able to pay pensions due to the lack of permission for banking operations after demonetisation
 8 se 14 november ke bich jo paise jamaa kiye gaye unke bare main kya upaay kiya jaae
 The economy related to the village has reached a high point
 is par supreme court ne atorni general se kaha he ki aap bataaen ki inhen kyon nahin dekh rahe hai
 Then the Attorney General said that his case is also being looked at but the difficulty is that the infrastructure of cooperative banks is not good
 inke paas niyamit bainkon kii tarah computerigeshan se lekar anya suvidhaayen nahin he ki jaali noton kii pahchaan ho sake or blike mani se bachaav ho sake
 In such a situation, these banks have been kept away from banking transactions for the same reason
 tippaniyan At the same time, Senior Advocate P
 presented on behalf of the petitioners
 chidambaram ne kaha ki desh bhar main 371 kooparative bank hai or is kaaran arthvyavastha par asar ho rahaa he
 Meanwhile, the Attorney General raised the issue of transfer of all the cases and said that the petitionation file is being filed in the daily demonetisation case across the country
 desh bhar main aise 70 arji daakhil ho chuke hai, supreme court main 15 argiyaan daakhil kii gai he
 In such a case, all the cases should be transferred to a High Court
 is par chif justise ties thakur ne kaha ki adaalatein hongi or maamle honge to court main log aaenge hi
 1
 notebandi kaa faisla RBI act 26 (2) kaa ulanghan he? jisamen kaha gaya he ki kendriya board kii manjuuri se ye kiya ja saktaa he or kisi siries ke noton ko band kiya ja saktaa he
 2
 notebandi kaa 8 november or uske baad ke notification asanvaidhanik hai? 3
 notebandi samvidhan ke die samanta ke adhikaar anuchhed 14 or vyapaar karne kii aazaadee se sambandhit anuchhed 19 jaise moulik adhikaron kaa ulanghan hai? 4
 notebandi ke faisle ko bina taiyaari ke saath lagu kiya gaya jabaki naa to nai karency kaa sahi intjaam tha or naa hi desh bhar main cash pahunchane kaa? 5
 bainkon or ATM se paisa nikaalane kii seemaa tay karnaa logon ke adhikaron kaa hanan he ? 6 Is it not right to stop depositing old notes in district cooperative banks and withdrawing new rupees? 7
 Can a political party file a petition in the Supreme Court under a public interest litigation? sunwaayee ke dauraan centre sarkaar kii ore se AG mukul rohtagi ne sawaal uthaaya ki CPM jaisi raajnneetik party kaise janhit yachika daakhil kar sakati he? chif justise thakur ne kaha ki wo is maamle kii sunwaayee bhi karenge
 The Center told the Supreme Court that till now the old currency of 12 lakh crores has been accumulated
 vahiin pi chidambaram ne kaha ki jis tareeke ke intjaam hai, usase saaf he ki sarkaar ko nai karency chhapane me paanch maheene kaa vakt lagegaa
 The Supreme Court is holding an important hearing in the demonetization case
 pichhali sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne sarkaar se kaha tha ki vah kooparative bainkon kii maang par vichaar kare jisamen unhone kaha he ki unhen banking oparation kii ijaajat nahin di gai he
 The cooperative banks have said that they have not been allowed to conduct banking transactions, due to which the customers are facing difficulty and the account holders who are facing problems are neither able to withdraw money nor Are able to deposit sunwaayee ke dauraan kerala or maharashtra ke kooparative baikon kii ore se kaha gaya ki notebandi ke baad banking oparation kii ijaajat nahin hone ke kaaran vah khataadharakon ko pement nahin kar paa rahaa he or pension nahin de paa rahe hai
 What measures should be taken regarding the money deposited between 8 and 14 November
 gaanv se sambandhit iconomi badahaali par pahunch chuki he
 On this, the Supreme Court has asked the Attorney General to explain why you are not seeing them
 tab atorni general ne kaha ki inke maamle ko bhi dekha ja rahaa he lekin mushkil ye he ki kooparative bainkon kaa infrastracchar thik nahin he
 Like regular banks, they do not have facilities other than computerization to identify fake currency and prevent black money
 aise main isi kaaran hi in bainkon ko banking transction se dur rakhaa gaya he
 The comments vahiin yachikakartaon kii ore se pesh senior edwocket pi
 Chidambaram said that there are 371 cooperative banks across the country and this is affecting the economy
 isi bich atorni general ne tamaam keson ke transfar kaa mudda uthaaya or kaha ki desh bhar main rojaanaa notebandi maamle main pitishan file ho rahi he
 As many as 70 such applications have been filed across the country, 15 applications have been filed in the Supreme Court
 aise main tamaam maamle ko ek hai court transfar kiya janaa chahie
 On this, Chief Justice TS Thakur said that there will be courts and if there are cases, people will come to the court

 If you are always in tension with your office and you get to hear the scolding of the boss for many times, then we are telling you such tips that you will easily handle your office work by following it
 follow karen ye tips
 
 - sabase pehle apane sabhi kaamon kii list banaaen
 After this, prepare a list of the work that is most important
 jab aap jarurat ke hisaab se kaam karte hai to aapkaa kaam aasaani se ho jaataa he
 - Email, the work that you spend the most time managing
 isliye kaam ke dauraan thodaa samay nikaalte hue mail ke jawaab dene ke saath-saath gairajaruri mail ko delit karnaa kabhi nahin bhoolen
 Never be in a hurry to get rid of work
 kaam dhyaan se karen
 In the hurry, there are more chances of making mistakes, in which case, payment of 1 mistake may have to be made in future
 - koun sa kaam jaldi ho saktaa he pehle us kaam ko karen
 Doing this can save your time and you can handle the rest
 - ye behad jaruri tips he
 Whenever you are doing, it is not necessary that you say yes to every task, you should also learn to say 'no'
 kaam hameshaa apnikshamtaake aadhaar par hi chune
 By doing this, the work is completed on time
 - offis main jo bhi meeting ho rahi he uske bare main jaan len ki vah kis mudde par hogi
 So that if you are asked anything in the meeting, you can reply immediately
 - kaam karte-karte kabhi bhi soshal hona nahin bhoolen
 People working around you have a lot of influence on how you behave
 - stress lekar kisi kaam ko nahin karen
 Stress always makes it difficult rather than making your work easier
 - apane computer, laptop main sari chijen sahi tareeke se rakhen
 This will help you ease in work and save your time too
 - sabase aakhri or jaruri baat ki kaam ke dauraan kabhi aalsee nahin hon
 Even a little carelessness towards work can outweigh you

 The Sahara Group has received some relief from the Securities Appellate Tribunal (SAT)
 sat ne bhartiya pratibhuti evam vinimay board (sebi) dwaara sahaara mutual fund ko yojanaon ko band karne ke liye die gaye aadesh par sthagan de diya he
 The matter will be next heard on 26 April
 sahaara samooh ne ek bayaan main kaha ki sebi ne pichley saptaah jari aadesh main sahaara mutual funds ko apni sabhi yojanaayen band karne ko kaha tha
 The SEBI order had said that all schemes, except one, should be closed by 21 April
 haalanki, company ko sahaara tex gen fund yojana 27 july tak jari rakhane kii anumati di gai thi, lekin is dauraan vah nayaa niveshak sweekaar nahin kar sakati thi
 As per SEBI order, the scheme was to be discontinued by 27 August
 sebi ke aadesh ko sahaara mutual fund ne nyaayaadhikaran main chunauti di thi
 The statement said that while giving relief to Sahara, the SAT has suspended the order of Sebi Sahara Mutual Fund to discontinue all its schemes except the tax gain fund
 sahaara samooh, sebi ke saath niamkeey or kanoonee ladaai main ulajhaa hua he
 The two units of Sahara are to be returned to the investors by Rs 24,000 crore
 july, 2015 main sebi ne sahaara emef kaa panjikaran radd karte hue kaha tha ki vah is kaarobaar ke liye upyukt nahin he
 The company was asked to transfer its operations to another MF company
 sebi ne chah maah kii avadhi samaapt hone ke baad sahaara emef ke panjikaran ko radd karne kaa aadesh diya tha
 Sahara MF appealed to the Securities Appellate Tribunal following the SEBI order which gave him six weeks to go to the Supreme Court
 company kii apil ko ucchtam nyaayalay ne aktubar, 2017 ko khaarij kar diya tha
 The comments iske baad sebi ne sahaara emef ko july, 2015 ke aadesh kii seemaa kaa kadai se paalan karne ko kaha tha
 Last week, Sebi amended its previous order directing Sahara MF to discontinue other schemes except Sahara Tax Gain Fund by 21 April 2018

 sahaara kii do ikaayiyon ko niveshkon kaa 24,000 karod rupee lautaanaa he
